\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Evaluators\ have\ to\ be\ specialized\ with\ respect\ to\ various\ criteria\ such\ as:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ storage/structure/shape}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ scalar\ type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ -\/\ etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Therefore,\ we\ need\ specialization\ of\ evaluator\ providing\ additional\ template\ arguments\ for\ each\ kind\ of\ evaluators.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ We\ currently\ distinguish\ the\ following\ kind\ of\ evaluators:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ unary\_evaluator\ \ \ \ for\ expressions\ taking\ only\ one\ arguments\ (CwiseUnaryOp,\ CwiseUnaryView,\ Transpose,\ MatrixWrapper,\ ArrayWrapper,\ Reverse,\ Replicate)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ binary\_evaluator\ \ \ for\ expression\ taking\ two\ arguments\ (CwiseBinaryOp)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ ternary\_evaluator\ \ \ for\ expression\ taking\ three\ arguments\ (CwiseTernaryOp)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ product\_evaluator\ \ for\ linear\ algebra\ products\ (Product);\ special\ case\ of\ binary\_evaluator\ because\ it\ requires\ additional\ tags\ for\ dispatching.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ mapbase\_evaluator\ \ for\ Map,\ Block,\ Ref}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ block\_evaluator\ \ \ \ for\ Block\ (special\ dispatching\ to\ a\ mapbase\_evaluator\ or\ unary\_evaluator)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00398\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ but\ this\ piece\ of\ code\ might\ still\ become\ handly\ if\ some\ other\ weird\ compilation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00399\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ erros\ pop\ up\ again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00400\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00401\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ MSVC\ exhibits\ a\ weird\ compilation\ error\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00402\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ compiling:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00403\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ Eigen::MatrixXf\ A\ =\ MatrixXf::Random(3,3);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00404\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ Ref<const\ MatrixXf>\ R\ =\ 2.f*A;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00405\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ that\ has\_*ary\_operator<scalar\_constant\_op<float>>\ have\ not\ been\ instantiated\ yet.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00406\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ "{}problem"{}\ is\ that\ evaluator<2.f*A>\ is\ instantiated\ by\ traits<Ref>::match<2.f*A>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00407\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ at\ that\ time\ has\_*ary\_operator<T>\ returns\ true\ regardless\ of\ T.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00408\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Then\ nullary\_wrapper\ is\ badly\ instantiated\ as\ nullary\_wrapper<.,.,true,true,true>.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00409\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ trick\ is\ thus\ to\ defer\ the\ proper\ instantiation\ of\ nullary\_wrapper\ when\ coeff(),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00410\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ packet()\ are\ really\ instantiated\ as\ implemented\ below:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00411\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00412\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ is\ a\ simple\ wrapper\ around\ Index\ to\ enforce\ the\ re-\/instantiation\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00413\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ has\_*ary\_operator\ when\ needed.}}
